 soochna kaa adhikaar (artiai) adhinium main sanshodhan kar centre do buniyadi tatwon ko badalanaa chaahati he
 The first is that the Information Commission's stature should be reduced from the Election Commission (EC) and control over change should be strengthened over a 5-year term
 india today ke paas sarkaar dwaara prastaavit sanshodhan kii copy he, jisase is baat kii pushti ho gai he ki sarkaar chunaav ayog ke mukaable soochna ayog ke aalaa adhikariyon ke vetan, bhatte or seva sharton kii samanta ko samaapt karne ja rahi he

 According to the proposed amendment, 'salaries and allowances payable to the Chief Information Commissioner and Information Commissioners and other terms and conditions may be determined by the Central Government
 'saath hi anya sanshodhan kaa lakshya mukhya soochna ayukta or anya rajyon ke soochna ayuktaon ke nirdhaarit paanch saal ke kaarykaal ko sanshodhit kar centre sarkaar dwaara nirdhaarit sharton main tabdeel karnaa he
 The government has clarified the bill to justify the amendment
 sarkaar kaa kahana he ki chunaav ayog or soochna ayog ke kaaryon main antar he
 The clarification states, 'the Election Commission is a constitutional body established by clause (1) of Article 324 of the Constitution, while the CIC and the State Information Commission are statutory bodies established under the provisions of the RTI Act, 2005
 'sarkaar kaa yah tark he ki mukhya soochna ayukta, soochna ayukta or rajyon ke soochna ayuktaon ko milane vaale vetan, bhatta or anya suvidhaayen mukhya chunaav ayukta, anya chunaav ayuktaon, rajya ke mukhya sachiv ke baraabar hai
 Whereas, the functions are different
 aisi sthiti main unke vetan or seva main tarksangat badlaav kii aavashyaktaa he

 unhone kaha ki soochna ke adhikaar ke bina vot kaa adhikaar bekaar he, kyonki donon ek duusare se jude hai
 This is the reason why the tenure of the Chief Election Commissioner, Chief Information Commissioner and Supreme Court judge and the process of removal from the post were kept equal
 unhone kaha ki sarkaar artiai adhinium kii neenv ko kamjor karne ke liye ek apaardarshee tareeke se kaam kar rahi he jise paardarshita or javabdehi ke nazariye se mahatvapurn kadam mana jaataa he
 Professor Ansari said, 'CIC was kept equal to others because of their work
 jiske tahat ve varishthata ke aadhaar par adhikariyon or anya logon ko notice jari kar sakate hai, jaankaree maang sakate hai
 But as soon as their salary is reduced, their position will also fall compared to the rest of the officers
